< Text>
Authentic middle eastern food, drink, and of course hookah.

They do things the old school way with wood coals that burn clean and built in ice chambers in their hookahs for a smooth puff from start to finish. I've always been impressed but last night was the first time I've been there since their remodel.

I absolutely love the new decor. It really opened the place up and makes it so much more inviting.

I had the chicken kebab and it was the best I've had (and I've had a lot).

This place is also open late, so it makes for a great after hours spot in Gaslamp. Unlike other hookah spots that try to be clubs, this place is a good mix of energy without the rowdyness.

Long story short, great food, great ambiance, great hookah.< /Text>

Staff is super friendly. Lots of great products. I frequent this store for the self service dog bathing. Reasonably priced at $10.
